of 4-bit\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#previous-news\"\u003ePrevious News\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-what-is-transformer-engine\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhat is Transformer Engine?\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-what-is-transformer-engine\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: What is Transformer Engine?\" href=\"#what-is-transformer-engine\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTransformer Engine (TE) is a library for accelerating Transformer models on NVIDIA GPUs, including\nusing 8-bit floating point (FP8) precision on Hopper, Ada, and Blackwell GPUs, to provide better\nperformance with lower memory utilization in both training and inference. TE provides a collection\nof highly optimized building blocks for popular Transformer architectures and an automatic mixed\nprecision-like API that can be used seamlessly with your framework-specific code. TE also includes a\nframework agnostic C++ API that can be integrated with other deep learning libraries to enable FP8\nsupport for Transformers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAs the number of parameters in Transformer models continues to grow, training and inference for\narchitectures such as BERT, GPT and T5 become very memory and compute-intensive. Most deep learning\nframeworks train with FP32 by default. This is not essential, however, to achieve full accuracy for\nmany deep learning models. Using mixed-precision training, which combines single-precision (FP32)\nwith lower precision (e.g. FP16) format when training a model, results in significant speedups with\nminimal differences in accuracy as compared to FP32 training. With Hopper GPU\narchitecture FP8 precision was introduced, which offers improved performance over FP16 with no\ndegradation in accuracy. Although all major deep learning frameworks support FP16, FP8 support is\nnot available natively in frameworks today.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTE addresses the problem of FP8 support by providing APIs that integrate with popular Large Language\nModel (LLM) libraries. It provides a Python API consisting of modules to easily build a Transformer\nlayer as well as a framework-agnostic library in C++ including structs and kernels needed for FP8\nsupport. Modules provided by TE internally maintain scaling factors and other values needed for FP8\ntraining, greatly simplifying mixed precision training for users.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-highlights\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eHighlights\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-highlights\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Highlights\" href=\"#highlights\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEasy-to-use modules for building Transformer layers with FP8 support\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOptimizations (e.g. fused kernels) for Transformer models\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupport for FP8 on NVIDIA Hopper, Ada, and Blackwell GPUs\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupport for optimizations across all precisions (FP16, BF16) on NVIDIA Ampere GPU architecture generations and later\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-id1\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eExamples\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-examples\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Examples\" href=\"#examples\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" models.\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003evariables\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese environment variables can be set before installation to customize the build process:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCUDA_PATH\u003c/strong\u003e: Path to CUDA installation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCUDNN_PATH\u003c/strong\u003e: Path to cuDNN parallel build jobs (default varies by system)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNVTE_BUILD_THREADS_PER_JOB\u003c/strong\u003e: Control threads per build job\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNVTE_CUDA_ARCHS\u003c/strong\u003e: Semicolon-separated list of CUDA compute architectures to compile for (e.g., \u003ccode\u003e80;90\u003c/code\u003e for A100 and H100). If not set, automatically determined based on CUDA version. Setting this can significantly reduce build time and binary size.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-compiling-with-flashattention\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eCompiling with FlashAttention\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-compiling-with-flashattention\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Compiling with FlashAttention\" href=\"#compiling-with-flashattention\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTransformer Engine supports both FlashAttention-2 and FlashAttention-3 in PyTorch for improved performance. FlashAttention-3 was added in release v1.11 and is prioritized over FlashAttention-2 when both are present in the environment.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can verify which FlashAttention version is being used by setting these environment variables:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"NVTE_DEBUG=1 NVTE_DEBUG_LEVEL=1 python your_script.py\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003eNVTE_DEBUG=1 NVTE_DEBUG_LEVEL=1 python your_script.py\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIt is a known issue that FlashAttention-2 compilation is resource-intensive and requires a large amount of RAM (see \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/Dao-AILab/flash-attention/issues/358\" data-hovercard-type=\"issue\" data-hovercard-url=\"/Dao-AILab/flash-attention/issues/358/hovercard\"\u003ebug\u003c/a\u003e), which may lead to out of memory errors during the installation of Transformer Engine. Please try setting \u003cstrong\u003eMAX_JOBS=1\u003c/strong\u003e in the environment to circumvent the issue.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-troubleshooting\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eTroubleshooting\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-troubleshooting\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Troubleshooting\" href=\"#troubleshooting\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCommon Issues and Solutions:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eABI Compatibility Issues:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSymptoms:\u003c/strong\u003e \u003ccode\u003eImportError\u003c/code\u003e with undefined symbols when importing transformer_engine\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolution:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure PyTorch and Transformer Engine are built with the same C++ ABI setting. Rebuild PyTorch from source with matching ABI.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eContext:\u003c/strong\u003e If you're using PyTorch built with a different C++ ABI than your system's default, you may encounter these undefined symbol errors. \u003ccode\u003envidia-cudnn-cu12/cu13\u003c/code\u003e. Use \u003ccode\u003e-v\u003c/code\u003e for verbose output to verify that TE is not pulling in a mismatching version of PyTorch or JAX that differs from the UV environment's version.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eJAX-specific Common Issues and Solutions:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFFI Issues:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSymptoms:\u003c/strong\u003e \u003ccode\u003eNo registered implementation for custom call to \u0026lt;some_te_ffi\u0026gt; for platform CUDA\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolution:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure \u003ccode\u003e--no-build-isolation\u003c/code\u003e is used during installation. If pre-building wheels, ensure that the wheel is both built and installed with \u003ccode\u003e--no-build-isolation\u003c/code\u003e. See \"Problems using UV or Virtual Environments\" above if using UV.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003ca viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-v1-7-padding-mask-definition-for-pytorch\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ev1.7: Padding mask definition for PyTorch\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-v17-padding-mask-definition-for-pytorch\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: v1.7: Padding mask definition for PyTorch\" href=\"#v17-padding-mask-definition-for-pytorch\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn an effort to unify the definition and usage of the attention mask across all three frameworks in Transformer Engine, the padding mask has changed from True meaning inclusion of the corresponding position in attention to exclusion of that position in our PyTorch implementation. Since v1.7, all attention mask types follow the same definition where True means masking out the corresponding position and False means including that position in attention calculation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAn example of this change is,\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# for a batch of 3 sequences where `a`s, `b`s and `c`s are the useful tokens\n# and `0`s are the padding tokens,\n[a, a, a, 0, 0,\n b, b, 0, 0, 0,\n c, c, c, c, 0]\n# the padding mask for this batch before v1.7 is,\n[ True,  True,  True, False, False,\n  True,  True, False, False, False,\n  True,  True,  True,  True, False]\n# and for v1.7 onwards it should be,\n[False, False, False,  True,  True,\n False, False,  True,  True,  True,\n False, False, False, False,  True]\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e for a batch of 3 sequences where `a`s, `b`s and `c`s are the useful tokens\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e and `0`s are the padding tokens,\u003c/span\u003e\n[a, a, a, 0, 0,\n b, b, 0, 0, 0,\n c, c, c, c, 0]\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e the padding mask for this batch before v1.7 is,\u003c/span\u003e\n[ True,  True,  True, False, False,\n  True,  True, False, False, False,\n  True,  True,  True,  True, False]\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e and for v1.7 onwards it should be,\u003c/span\u003e\n[False, False, False,  True,  True,\n False, False,  True,  True,  True,\n False, False, False, False,  True]\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003ca name=\"user-content-id3\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" aria-label=\"Permalink: FP8 Convergence\" href=\"#fp8-convergence\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" found \u003cstrong\u003eno significant difference\u003c/strong\u003e between FP8 and BF16 training loss curves. FP8 has also been validated for accuracy on downstream LLM tasks (e.g. LAMBADA and WikiText). <a name="user-content-what-is-transformer-engine"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What is Transformer Engine?</h2><a id="user-content-what-is-transformer-engine" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What is Transformer Engine?" href="#what-is-transformer-engine"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Transformer Engine (TE) is a library for accelerating Transformer models on NVIDIA GPUs, including
using 8-bit floating point (FP8) precision on Hopper, Ada, and Blackwell GPUs, to provide better
performance with lower memory utilization in both training and inference. TE provides a collection
of highly optimized building blocks for popular Transformer architectures and an automatic mixed
precision-like API that can be used seamlessly with your framework-specific code. TE also includes a
framework agnostic C++ API that can be integrated with other deep learning libraries to enable FP8
support for Transformers.</p>
<p dir="auto">As the number of parameters in Transformer models continues to grow, training and inference for
architectures such as BERT, GPT and T5 become very memory and compute-intensive. Most deep learning
frameworks train with FP32 by default. This is not essential, however, to achieve full accuracy for
many deep learning models. Using mixed-precision training, which combines single-precision (FP32)
with lower precision (e.g. FP16) format when training a model, results in significant speedups with
minimal differences in accuracy as compared to FP32 training. With Hopper GPU
architecture FP8 precision was introduced, which offers improved performance over FP16 with no
degradation in accuracy. Although all major deep learning frameworks support FP16, FP8 support is
not available natively in frameworks today.</p>
<p dir="auto">TE addresses the problem of FP8 support by providing APIs that integrate with popular Large Language
Model (LLM) libraries. It provides a Python API consisting of modules to easily build a Transformer
layer as well as a framework-agnostic library in C++ including structs and kernels needed for FP8
support. Modules provided by TE internally maintain scaling factors and other values needed for FP8
training, greatly simplifying mixed precision training for users.</p>
<a name="user-content-highlights"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Highlights</h2><a id="user-content-highlights" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Highlights" href="#highlights"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Easy-to-use modules for building Transformer layers with FP8 support</li>
<li>Optimizations (e.g. fused kernels) for Transformer models</li>
<li>Support for FP8 on NVIDIA Hopper, Ada, and Blackwell GPUs</li>
<li>Support for optimizations across all precisions (FP16, BF16) on NVIDIA Ampere GPU architecture generations and later</li>
</ul>
<a name="user-content-id1"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Examples</h2><a id="user-content-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Examples" href="#examples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">PyTorch</h3><a id="user-content-pytorch" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: PyTorch" href="#pytorch"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import torch
import transformer_engine.pytorch as te
from transformer_engine.common import recipe

# Set dimensions.
in_features = 768
out_features = 3072
hidden_size = 2048

# Initialize model and inputs.
model = te.Linear(in_features, out_features, bias=True)
inp = torch.randn(hidden_size, in_features, device=&quot;cuda&quot;)

# Create an FP8 recipe. Note: All input args are optional.
fp8_recipe = recipe.DelayedScaling(margin=0, fp8_format=recipe.Format.E4M3)

# Enable autocasting for the forward pass
with te.autocast(enabled=True, recipe=fp8_recipe):
    out = model(inp)

loss = out.sum()
loss.backward()"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>

<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">transformer_engine</span>.<span class="pl-s1">common</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">recipe</span>

<span class="pl-c"># Set dimensions.</span>

<span class="pl-s1">hidden_size</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2048</span>

<span class="pl-c"># Initialize model and inputs.</span>

    <span class="pl-s1">out</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">model</span>(<span class="pl-s1">inp</span>)

<span class="pl-s1">loss</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">out</span>.<span class="pl-c1">sum</span>()

<a name="user-content-jax"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">JAX</h3><a id="user-content-jax" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: JAX" href="#jax"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<a name="user-content-flax"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Flax</h4><a id="user-content-flax" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Flax" href="#flax"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import flax
import jax
import jax.numpy as jnp
import transformer_engine.jax as te
import transformer_engine.jax.flax as te_flax
from transformer_engine.common import recipe

BATCH = 32
SEQLEN = 128
HIDDEN = 1024

# Initialize RNG and inputs.
rng = jax.random.PRNGKey(0)
init_rng, data_rng = jax.random.split(rng)
inp = jax.random.normal(data_rng, [BATCH, SEQLEN, HIDDEN], jnp.float32)

# Create an FP8 recipe. Note: All input args are optional.
fp8_recipe = recipe.DelayedScaling(margin=0, fp8_format=recipe.Format.HYBRID)

# Enable autocasting for the forward pass
with te.autocast(enabled=True, recipe=fp8_recipe):
    model = te_flax.DenseGeneral(features=HIDDEN)

    def loss_fn(params, other_vars, inp):
      out = model.apply({'params':params, **other_vars}, inp)
      return jnp.mean(out)

    # Initialize models.
    variables = model.init(init_rng, inp)
    other_variables, params = flax.core.pop(variables, 'params')

    # Construct the forward and backward function
    fwd_bwd_fn = jax.value_and_grad(loss_fn, argnums=(0, 1))

    for _ in range(10):
      loss, (param_grads, other_grads) = fwd_bwd_fn(params, other_variables, inp)"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">flax</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">jax</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">jax</span>.<span class="pl-s1">numpy</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">jnp</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">transformer_engine</span>.<span class="pl-s1">jax</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">te</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">transformer_engine</span>.<span class="pl-s1">jax</span>.<span class="pl-s1">flax</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">te_flax</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">transformer_engine</span>.<span class="pl-s1">common</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">recipe</span>

<span class="pl-c1">BATCH</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">32</span>
<span class="pl-c1">SEQLEN</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">128</span>
<span class="pl-c1">HIDDEN</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1024</span>

<span class="pl-c"># Initialize RNG and inputs.</span>
<span class="pl-s1">rng</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">jax</span>.<span class="pl-c1">random</span>.<span class="pl-c1">PRNGKey</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
<span class="pl-s1">init_rng</span>, <span class="pl-s1">data_rng</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">jax</span>.<span class="pl-c1">random</span>.<span class="pl-c1">split</span>(<span class="pl-s1">rng</span>)
<span class="pl-s1">inp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">jax</span>.<span class="pl-c1">random</span>.<span class="pl-c1">normal</span>(<span class="pl-s1">data_rng</span>, [<span class="pl-c1">BATCH</span>, <span class="pl-c1">SEQLEN</span>, <span class="pl-c1">HIDDEN</span>], <span class="pl-s1">jnp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">float32</span>)

<span class="pl-c"># Create an FP8 recipe. Note: All input args are optional.</span>
<span class="pl-s1">fp8_recipe</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">recipe</span>.<span class="pl-c1">DelayedScaling</span>(<span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-s1">fp8_format</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">recipe</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Format</span>.<span class="pl-c1">HYBRID</span>)

<span class="pl-c"># Enable autocasting for the forward pass</span>
<span class="pl-k">with</span> <span class="pl-s1">te</span>.<span class="pl-c1">autocast</span>(<span class="pl-s1">enabled</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>, <span class="pl-s1">recipe</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">fp8_recipe</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">model</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">te_flax</span>.<span class="pl-c1">DenseGeneral</span>(<span class="pl-s1">features</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">HIDDEN</span>)

    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">loss_fn</span>(<span class="pl-s1">params</span>, <span class="pl-s1">other_vars</span>, <span class="pl-s1">inp</span>):
      <span class="pl-s1">out</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">model</span>.<span class="pl-c1">apply</span>({<span class="pl-s">'params'</span>:<span class="pl-s1">params</span>, <span class="pl-c1">**</span><span class="pl-s1">other_vars</span>}, <span class="pl-s1">inp</span>)
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">jnp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mean</span>(<span class="pl-s1">out</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># Initialize models.</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">variables</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">model</span>.<span class="pl-c1">init</span>(<span class="pl-s1">init_rng</span>, <span class="pl-s1">inp</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">other_variables</span>, <span class="pl-s1">params</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">flax</span>.<span class="pl-c1">core</span>.<span class="pl-c1">pop</span>(<span class="pl-s1">variables</span>, <span class="pl-s">'params'</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># Construct the forward and backward function</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">fwd_bwd_fn</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">jax</span>.<span class="pl-c1">value_and_grad</span>(<span class="pl-s1">loss_fn</span>, <span class="pl-s1">argnums</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>))

    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">_</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>):
      <span class="pl-s1">loss</span>, (<span class="pl-s1">param_grads</span>, <span class="pl-s1">other_grads</span>) <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">fwd_bwd_fn</span>(<span class="pl-s1">params</span>, <span class="pl-s1">other_variables</span>, <span class="pl-s1">inp</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For a more comprehensive tutorial, check out our <a href="https://docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/transformer-engine/user-guide/getting_started.html" rel="nofollow">Getting Started Guide</a>.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<a name="user-content-system-requirements"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">System Requirements</h3><a id="user-content-system-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: System Requirements" href="#system-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Hardware:</strong> Blackwell, Hopper, Grace Hopper/Blackwell, Ada, Ampere</li>
<li><strong>OS:</strong> Linux (official), WSL2 (limited support)</li>
<li><strong>Software:</strong><ul dir="auto">
<li>CUDA: 12.1+ (Hopper/Ada/Ampere), 12.8+ (Blackwell) with compatible NVIDIA drivers</li>
<li>cuDNN: 9.3+</li>
<li>Compiler: GCC 9+ or Clang 10+ with C++17 support</li>
<li>Python: 3.12 recommended</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Source Build Requirements:</strong> CMake 3.18+, Ninja, Git 2.17+, pybind11 2.6.0+</li>
<li><strong>Notes:</strong> FP8 features require Compute Capability 8.9+ (Ada/Hopper/Blackwell)</li>
</ul>
<a name="user-content-installation-methods"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation Methods</h3><a id="user-content-installation-methods" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation Methods" href="#installation-methods"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<a name="user-content-docker-recommended"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Docker (Recommended)</h3><a id="user-content-docker-recommended" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Docker (Recommended)" href="#docker-recommended"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The quickest way to get started with Transformer Engine is by using Docker images on
<a href="https://catalog.ngc.nvidia.com/orgs/nvidia/containers/pytorch" rel="nofollow">NVIDIA GPU Cloud (NGC) Catalog</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">For example to use the NGC PyTorch container interactively,</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker run --gpus all -it --rm nvcr.io/nvidia/pytorch:26.01-py3"><pre>docker run --gpus all -it --rm nvcr.io/nvidia/pytorch:26.01-py3</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For example to use the NGC JAX container interactively,</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker run --gpus all -it --rm nvcr.io/nvidia/jax:26.01-py3"><pre>docker run --gpus all -it --rm nvcr.io/nvidia/jax:26.01-py3</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Where 26.01 (corresponding to January 2026 release) is the container version.</p>
<p dir="auto">We recommend updating to the latest NGC container available here:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://catalog.ngc.nvidia.com/orgs/nvidia/containers/pytorch" rel="nofollow">https://catalog.ngc.nvidia.com/orgs/nvidia/containers/pytorch</a></li>
<li><a href="https://catalog.ngc.nvidia.com/orgs/nvidia/containers/jax" rel="nofollow">https://catalog.ngc.nvidia.com/orgs/nvidia/containers/jax</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">If you run any examples, please ensure you are using a matching version of TransformerEngine. TransformerEngine is pre-built and packaged inside the containers with examples available at <code>/opt/transformerengine</code> or <code>/opt/transformer-engine</code>. If you would like to use examples from TE main branch and are running into import errors, please try the latest pip package or building from source, although NGC containers are recommended for ease-of-use for most users.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Benefits of using NGC containers:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>All dependencies pre-installed with compatible versions and optimized configurations</li>
<li>NGC PyTorch 23.08+ containers include FlashAttention-2</li>
</ul>
<a name="user-content-pip-installation"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">pip Installation</h3><a id="user-content-pip-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: pip Installation" href="#pip-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Prerequisites for pip installation:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A compatible C++ compiler</li>
<li>CUDA Toolkit with cuDNN and NVCC (NVIDIA CUDA Compiler) if installing from source.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">To install the latest stable version with pip:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# For PyTorch integration
pip install --no-build-isolation transformer_engine[pytorch]

# For JAX integration
pip install --no-build-isolation transformer_engine[jax]

# For both frameworks
pip install --no-build-isolation transformer_engine[pytorch,jax]"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For PyTorch integration</span>
pip install --no-build-isolation transformer_engine[pytorch]

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For JAX integration</span>
pip install --no-build-isolation transformer_engine[jax]

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For both frameworks</span>
pip install --no-build-isolation transformer_engine[pytorch,jax]</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, install directly from the GitHub repository:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip install --no-build-isolation git+https://github.com/NVIDIA/TransformerEngine.git@stable"><pre>pip install --no-build-isolation git+https://github.com/NVIDIA/TransformerEngine.git@stable</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">When installing from GitHub, you can explicitly specify frameworks using the environment variable:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="NVTE_FRAMEWORK=pytorch,jax pip install --no-build-isolation git+https://github.com/NVIDIA/TransformerEngine.git@stable"><pre>NVTE_FRAMEWORK=pytorch,jax pip install --no-build-isolation git+https://github.com/NVIDIA/TransformerEngine.git@stable</pre></div>
<a name="user-content-conda-installation"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">conda Installation</h3><a id="user-content-conda-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: conda Installation" href="#conda-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To install the latest stable version with conda from conda-forge:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# For PyTorch integration
conda install -c conda-forge transformer-engine-torch

# JAX integration (coming soon)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For PyTorch integration</span>
conda install -c conda-forge transformer-engine-torch

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> JAX integration (coming soon)</span></pre></div>
<a name="user-content-source-installation"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Source Installation</h3><a id="user-content-source-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Source Installation" href="#source-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/transformer-engine/user-guide/installation.html#installation-from-source" rel="nofollow">See the installation guide</a></p>
<a name="user-content-environment-variables"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Environment Variables</h3><a id="user-content-environment-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Environment Variables" href="#environment-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These environment variables can be set before installation to customize the build process:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>CUDA_PATH</strong>: Path to CUDA installation</li>
<li><strong>CUDNN_PATH</strong>: Path to cuDNN installation</li>
<li><strong>CXX</strong>: Path to C++ compiler</li>
<li><strong>NVTE_FRAMEWORK</strong>: Comma-separated list of frameworks to build for (e.g., <code>pytorch,jax</code>)</li>
<li><strong>MAX_JOBS</strong>: Limit number of parallel build jobs (default varies by system)</li>
<li><strong>NVTE_BUILD_THREADS_PER_JOB</strong>: Control threads per build job</li>
<li><strong>NVTE_CUDA_ARCHS</strong>: Semicolon-separated list of CUDA compute architectures to compile for (e.g., <code>80;90</code> for A100 and H100). If not set, automatically determined based on CUDA version. Setting this can significantly reduce build time and binary size.</li>
</ul>
<a name="user-content-compiling-with-flashattention"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compiling with FlashAttention</h3><a id="user-content-compiling-with-flashattention" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compiling with FlashAttention" href="#compiling-with-flashattention"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Transformer Engine supports both FlashAttention-2 and FlashAttention-3 in PyTorch for improved performance. FlashAttention-3 was added in release v1.11 and is prioritized over FlashAttention-2 when both are present in the environment.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can verify which FlashAttention version is being used by setting these environment variables:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="NVTE_DEBUG=1 NVTE_DEBUG_LEVEL=1 python your_script.py"><pre>NVTE_DEBUG=1 NVTE_DEBUG_LEVEL=1 python your_script.py</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">It is a known issue that FlashAttention-2 compilation is resource-intensive and requires a large amount of RAM (see <a href="https://github.com/Dao-AILab/flash-attention/issues/358" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/Dao-AILab/flash-attention/issues/358/hovercard">bug</a>), which may lead to out of memory errors during the installation of Transformer Engine. Please try setting <strong>MAX_JOBS=1</strong> in the environment to circumvent the issue.</p>
<a name="user-content-troubleshooting"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Troubleshooting</h3><a id="user-content-troubleshooting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Troubleshooting" href="#troubleshooting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Common Issues and Solutions:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>ABI Compatibility Issues:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Symptoms:</strong> <code>ImportError</code> with undefined symbols when importing transformer_engine</li>
<li><strong>Solution:</strong> Ensure PyTorch and Transformer Engine are built with the same C++ ABI setting. Rebuild PyTorch from source with matching ABI.</li>
<li><strong>Context:</strong> If you're using PyTorch built with a different C++ ABI than your system's default, you may encounter these undefined symbol errors. This is particularly common with pip-installed PyTorch outside of containers.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Missing Headers or Libraries:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Symptoms:</strong> CMake errors about missing headers (<code>cudnn.h</code>, <code>cublas_v2.h</code>, <code>filesystem</code>, etc.)</p>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Solution:</strong> Install missing development packages or set environment variables to point to correct locations:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export CUDA_PATH=/path/to/cuda
export CUDNN_PATH=/path/to/cudnn"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> CUDA_PATH=/path/to/cuda
<span class="pl-k">export</span> CUDNN_PATH=/path/to/cudnn</pre></div>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto">If CMake can't find a C++ compiler, set the <code>CXX</code> environment variable.</p>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto">Ensure all paths are correctly set before installation.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Build Resource Issues:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Symptoms:</strong> Compilation hangs, system freezes, or out-of-memory errors</p>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Solution:</strong> Limit parallel builds:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="MAX_JOBS=1 NVTE_BUILD_THREADS_PER_JOB=1 pip install ..."><pre>MAX_JOBS=1 NVTE_BUILD_THREADS_PER_JOB=1 pip install ...</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Verbose Build Logging:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><p dir="auto">For detailed build logs to help diagnose issues:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd transformer_engine
pip install -v -v -v --no-build-isolation ."><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> transformer_engine
pip install -v -v -v --no-build-isolation <span class="pl-c1">.</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problems using UV or Virtual Environments:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Import Error:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Symptoms:</strong> Cannot import <code>transformer_engine</code></li>
<li><strong>Solution:</strong> Ensure your UV environment is active and that you have used <code>uv pip install --no-build-isolation &lt;te_pypi_package_or_wheel_or_source_dir&gt;</code> instead of a regular pip install to your system environment.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>cuDNN Sublibrary Loading Failed:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Symptoms:</strong> Errors at runtime with <code>CUDNN_STATUS_SUBLIBRARY_LOADING_FAILED</code></p>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Solution:</strong> This can occur when TE is built against the container's system installation of cuDNN, but pip packages inside the virtual environment pull in pip packages for <code>nvidia-cudnn-cu12/cu13</code>. To resolve this, when building TE from source please specify the following environment variables to point to the cuDNN in your virtual environment.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export CUDNN_PATH=$(pwd)/.venv/lib/python3.12/site-packages/nvidia/cudnn
export CUDNN_HOME=$CUDNN_PATH
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$CUDNN_PATH/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> CUDNN_PATH=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>pwd<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>/.venv/lib/python3.12/site-packages/nvidia/cudnn
<span class="pl-k">export</span> CUDNN_HOME=<span class="pl-smi">$CUDNN_PATH</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> LD_LIBRARY_PATH=<span class="pl-smi">$CUDNN_PATH</span>/lib:<span class="pl-smi">$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p dir="auto"><strong>Building Wheels:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Symptoms:</strong> Regular TE installs work correctly but UV wheel builds fail at runtime.</li>
<li><strong>Solution:</strong> Ensure that <code>uv build --wheel --no-build-isolation -v</code> is used during the wheel build as well as the pip installation of the wheel. Use <code>-v</code> for verbose output to verify that TE is not pulling in a mismatching version of PyTorch or JAX that differs from the UV environment's version.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>JAX-specific Common Issues and Solutions:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>FFI Issues:</strong><ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Symptoms:</strong> <code>No registered implementation for custom call to &lt;some_te_ffi&gt; for platform CUDA</code></li>
<li><strong>Solution:</strong> Ensure <code>--no-build-isolation</code> is used during installation. If pre-building wheels, ensure that the wheel is both built and installed with <code>--no-build-isolation</code>. See "Problems using UV or Virtual Environments" above if using UV.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<a name="user-content-breaking-changes"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Breaking Changes</h2><a id="user-content-breaking-changes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Breaking Changes" href="#breaking-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<a name="user-content-v1-7-padding-mask-definition-for-pytorch"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v1.7: Padding mask definition for PyTorch</h3><a id="user-content-v17-padding-mask-definition-for-pytorch" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v1.7: Padding mask definition for PyTorch" href="#v17-padding-mask-definition-for-pytorch"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In an effort to unify the definition and usage of the attention mask across all three frameworks in Transformer Engine, the padding mask has changed from True meaning inclusion of the corresponding position in attention to exclusion of that position in our PyTorch implementation. Since v1.7, all attention mask types follow the same definition where True means masking out the corresponding position and False means including that position in attention calculation.</p>
<p dir="auto">An example of this change is,</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# for a batch of 3 sequences where `a`s, `b`s and `c`s are the useful tokens
# and `0`s are the padding tokens,
[a, a, a, 0, 0,
 b, b, 0, 0, 0,
 c, c, c, c, 0]
# the padding mask for this batch before v1.7 is,
[ True,  True,  True, False, False,
  True,  True, False, False, False,
  True,  True,  True,  True, False]
# and for v1.7 onwards it should be,
[False, False, False,  True,  True,
 False, False,  True,  True,  True,
 False, False, False, False,  True]"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> for a batch of 3 sequences where `a`s, `b`s and `c`s are the useful tokens</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> and `0`s are the padding tokens,</span>
[a, a, a, 0, 0,
 b, b, 0, 0, 0,
 c, c, c, c, 0]
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> the padding mask for this batch before v1.7 is,</span>
[ True,  True,  True, False, False,
  True,  True, False, False, False,
  True,  True,  True,  True, False]
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> and for v1.7 onwards it should be,</span>
[False, False, False,  True,  True,
 False, False,  True,  True,  True,
 False, False, False, False,  True]</pre></div>
<a name="user-content-id3"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">FP8 Convergence</h2><a id="user-content-fp8-convergence" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: FP8 Convergence" href="#fp8-convergence"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">FP8 has been tested extensively across different model architectures and configurations and we found <strong>no significant difference</strong> between FP8 and BF16 training loss curves. FP8 has also been validated for accuracy on downstream LLM tasks (e.g. LAMBADA and WikiText). Below are examples of models tested for convergence across different frameworks.</p>

<a name="user-content-id4"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Integrations</h2><a id="user-content-integrations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Integrations" href="#integrations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Transformer Engine has been integrated with popular LLM frameworks such as:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/deepspeedai/DeepSpeed/blob/master/tests/unit/runtime/half_precision/test_fp8.py">DeepSpeed</a></li>

<a name="user-content-contributing"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Contributing</h2><a id="user-content-contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contributing" href="#contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We welcome contributions to Transformer Engine! To contribute to Transformer Engine and make pull requests,
follow the guidelines outlined in the <a href="/NVIDIA/TransformerEngine/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.rst">CONTRIBUTING.rst</a> guide.</p>

  <div class="BorderGrid-row">
    <div class="BorderGrid-cell">
      <div class="hide-sm hide-md">
  <h2 class="tmp-mb-3 h4">About</h2>

      <p class="f4 tmp-my-3">
        A library for accelerating Transformer models on NVIDIA GPUs, including using 8-bit and 4-bit floating point (FP8 and FP4) precision on Hopper, Ada and Blackwell GPUs, to provide better performance with lower memory utilization in both training and inference.
      </p>
      <div class="tmp-my-3 d-flex flex-items-center">
        <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-link flex-shrink-0 mr-2 tmp-mr-2">
    <path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path>
</svg>
        <span class="flex-auto min-width-0 css-truncate css-truncate-target width-fit">
          <a title="https://docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/transformer-engine/user-guide/index.html" role="link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" class="text-bold" href="https://docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/transformer-engine/user-guide/index.html">docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/transformer-engine/user-guide/index.html</a>
        </span>
      </div>
